<Operation>

<OperationTitleSection slot="title">

## <Pill variant="primary"><b>GET</b></Pill> /v1/fine\_tuning/jobs \{#operation-jobs_api_routes_fine_tuning_get_fine_tuning_jobs\}

</OperationTitleSection>

<OperationSummarySection slot="summary">

_Get Fine Tuning Jobs_

</OperationSummarySection>

<OperationDescriptionSection slot="description">

Get a list of fine-tuning jobs for your organization and user.

</OperationDescriptionSection>

<OperationCodeSamplesSection slot="code-samples">

<CodeSampleTabbedSection>

<CodeSampleTab
  slot="tab"
  id="operation-jobs_api_routes_fine_tuning_get_fine_tuning_jobs_code-samples_typescript"
  tags={{"codeSample":"typescript"}}
>

TypeScript

</CodeSampleTab>

<SectionContent
  slot="content"
  id="operation-jobs_api_routes_fine_tuning_get_fine_tuning_jobs_code-samples_typescript"
>

<CodeSample>

```typescript
import { Mistral } from "@mistralai/mistralai";

const mistral = new Mistral({
  apiKey: "MISTRAL_API_KEY",
});

async function run() {
  const result = await mistral.fineTuning.jobs.list({});

  console.log(result);
}

run();

```

</CodeSample>

</SectionContent>

<CodeSampleTab
  slot="tab"
  id="operation-jobs_api_routes_fine_tuning_get_fine_tuning_jobs_code-samples_python"
  tags={{"codeSample":"python"}}
>

Python

</CodeSampleTab>

<SectionContent
  slot="content"
  id="operation-jobs_api_routes_fine_tuning_get_fine_tuning_jobs_code-samples_python"
>

<CodeSample>

```python
from mistralai import Mistral
import os


with Mistral(
    api_key=os.getenv("MISTRAL_API_KEY", ""),
) as mistral:

    res = mistral.fine_tuning.jobs.list(page=0, page_size=100, created_by_me=False)

    # Handle response
    print(res)


```

</CodeSample>

</SectionContent>

<CodeSampleTab
  slot="tab"
  id="operation-jobs_api_routes_fine_tuning_get_fine_tuning_jobs_code-samples_curl"
  tags={{"codeSample":"curl"}}

cURL

<CodeSample>

```curl
curl https://api.mistral.ai/v1/fine_tuning/jobs \
 -X GET \
 -H 'Authorization: Bearer YOUR_APIKEY_HERE'
```

</CodeSample>

</SectionContent>

<Operation>

<OperationTitleSection slot="title">

## <Pill variant="primary"><b>POST</b></Pill> /v1/fine\_tuning/jobs \{#operation-jobs_api_routes_fine_tuning_create_fine_tuning_job\}

</OperationTitleSection>

<OperationSummarySection slot="summary">

_Create Fine Tuning Job_

</OperationSummarySection>

<OperationDescriptionSection slot="description">

Create a new fine-tuning job, it will be queued for processing.

</OperationDescriptionSection>

<OperationCodeSamplesSection slot="code-samples">

<CodeSampleTabbedSection>

<CodeSampleTab
  slot="tab"
  id="operation-jobs_api_routes_fine_tuning_create_fine_tuning_job_code-samples_typescript"
  tags={{"codeSample":"typescript"}}
>

TypeScript

</CodeSampleTab>

<SectionContent
  slot="content"
  id="operation-jobs_api_routes_fine_tuning_create_fine_tuning_job_code-samples_typescript"
>

<CodeSample>

```typescript
import { Mistral } from "@mistralai/mistralai";

const mistral = new Mistral({
  apiKey: "MISTRAL_API_KEY",
});

async function run() {
  const result = await mistral.fineTuning.jobs.create({
    model: "Camaro",
    hyperparameters: {
      learningRate: 0.0001,
    },
  });

  console.log(result);
}

run();

```

</CodeSample>

</SectionContent>

<CodeSampleTab
  slot="tab"
  id="operation-jobs_api_routes_fine_tuning_create_fine_tuning_job_code-samples_python"
  tags={{"codeSample":"python"}}
>

Python

</CodeSampleTab>

<SectionContent
  slot="content"
  id="operation-jobs_api_routes_fine_tuning_create_fine_tuning_job_code-samples_python"
>

<CodeSample>

```python
from mistralai import Mistral
import os


with Mistral(
    api_key=os.getenv("MISTRAL_API_KEY", ""),
) as mistral:

    res = mistral.fine_tuning.jobs.create(model="Camaro", hyperparameters={
        "learning_rate": 0.0001,
    }, invalid_sample_skip_percentage=0)

    # Handle response
    print(res)


```

</CodeSample>

</SectionContent>

<CodeSampleTab
  slot="tab"
  id="operation-jobs_api_routes_fine_tuning_create_fine_tuning_job_code-samples_curl"
  tags={{"codeSample":"curl"}}
>

cURL

</CodeSampleTab>

<SectionContent
  slot="content"
  id="operation-jobs_api_routes_fine_tuning_create_fine_tuning_job_code-samples_curl"
>

<CodeSample>

```curl
curl https://api.mistral.ai/v1/fine_tuning/jobs \
 -X POST \
 -H 'Authorization: Bearer YOUR_APIKEY_HERE' \
 -d '{
  "hyperparameters": {},
  "model": "ministral-3b-latest"
}'
```

</CodeSample>

</SectionContent>

</CodeSampleTabbedSection>

</OperationCodeSamplesSection>

  slot="entry"
  id="dry_run"
  headingId="operation-jobs_api_routes_fine_tuning_create_fine_tuning_job_parameters_dry_run"
  typeInfo={{"label":"union","linkedLabel":"union","children":[{"label":"boolean","linkedLabel":"boolean","children":[],"breakoutSubTypes":{}},{"label":"null","linkedLabel":"null","children":[],"breakoutSubTypes":{}}],"breakoutSubTypes":{}}}
  typeAnnotations={[{"title":"query","variant":"info"}]}
  hasExpandableContent={true}
  expandByDefault={false}
>

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### dry_run \{#operation-jobs_api_routes_fine_tuning_create_fine_tuning_job_parameters_dry_run\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

* If `true` the job is not spawned, instead the query returns a handful of useful metadata
  for the user to perform sanity checks (see `LegacyJobMetadataOut` response).
* Otherwise, the job is started and the query returns the job ID along with some of the
  input parameters (see `JobOut` response).


</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

</ExpandableProperty>

</ExpandableSection>

</SectionContent>

</Section>

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### training_steps \{#operation-jobs_api_routes_fine_tuning_create_fine_tuning_job_request_hyperparameters_completiontrainingparametersin_training_steps\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

The number of training steps to perform. A training step refers to a single update of the model weights during the fine-tuning process. This update is typically calculated using a batch of samples from the training dataset.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

</ExpandableProperty>

<ExpandableProperty
  slot="entry"
  id="hyperparameters_CompletionTrainingParametersIn_warmup_fraction"
  headingId="operation-jobs_api_routes_fine_tuning_create_fine_tuning_job_request_hyperparameters_completiontrainingparametersin_warmup_fraction"
  parentId="hyperparameters_CompletionTrainingParametersIn"
  typeInfo={{"label":"union","linkedLabel":"union","children":[{"label":"number","linkedLabel":"number","children":[],"breakoutSubTypes":{}},{"label":"null","linkedLabel":"null","children":[],"breakoutSubTypes":{}}],"breakoutSubTypes":{}}}
  typeAnnotations={[]}
  hasExpandableContent={true}
  expandByDefault={false}
>

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### warmup_fraction \{#operation-jobs_api_routes_fine_tuning_create_fine_tuning_job_request_hyperparameters_completiontrainingparametersin_warmup_fraction\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

(Advanced Usage) A parameter that specifies the percentage of the total training steps at which the learning rate warm-up phase ends. During this phase, the learning rate gradually increases from a small value to the initial learning rate, helping to stabilize the training process and improve convergence. Similar to `pct_start` in [mistral-finetune](https://github.com/mistralai/mistral-finetune)

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

</ExpandableProperty>

<ExpandableProperty
  slot="entry"
  id="hyperparameters_CompletionTrainingParametersIn_weight_decay"
  headingId="operation-jobs_api_routes_fine_tuning_create_fine_tuning_job_request_hyperparameters_completiontrainingparametersin_weight_decay"
  parentId="hyperparameters_CompletionTrainingParametersIn"
  typeInfo={{"label":"union","linkedLabel":"union","children":[{"label":"number","linkedLabel":"number","children":[],"breakoutSubTypes":{}},{"label":"null","linkedLabel":"null","children":[],"breakoutSubTypes":{}}],"breakoutSubTypes":{}}}
  typeAnnotations={[]}
  hasExpandableContent={true}
  expandByDefault={false}
>

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### weight_decay \{#operation-jobs_api_routes_fine_tuning_create_fine_tuning_job_request_hyperparameters_completiontrainingparametersin_weight_decay\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

(Advanced Usage) Weight decay adds a term to the loss function that is proportional to the sum of the squared weights. This term reduces the magnitude of the weights and prevents them from growing too large.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

</ExpandableProperty>

##### validation_files \{#operation-jobs_api_routes_fine_tuning_create_fine_tuning_job_request_validation_files\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

A list containing the IDs of uploaded files that contain validation data. If you provide these files, the data is used to generate validation metrics periodically during fine-tuning. These metrics can be viewed in `checkpoints` when getting the status of a running fine-tuning job. The same data should not be present in both train and validation files.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

<Operation>

<OperationTitleSection slot="title">

## <Pill variant="primary"><b>GET</b></Pill> /v1/fine\_tuning/jobs/\{job\_id\} \{#operation-jobs_api_routes_fine_tuning_get_fine_tuning_job\}

</OperationTitleSection>

<OperationSummarySection slot="summary">

_Get Fine Tuning Job_

</OperationSummarySection>

<OperationDescriptionSection slot="description">

Get a fine-tuned job details by its UUID.

</OperationDescriptionSection>

<OperationCodeSamplesSection slot="code-samples">

<CodeSampleTabbedSection>

<CodeSampleTab
  slot="tab"
  id="operation-jobs_api_routes_fine_tuning_get_fine_tuning_job_code-samples_typescript"
  tags={{"codeSample":"typescript"}}
>

TypeScript

</CodeSampleTab>

<SectionContent
  slot="content"
  id="operation-jobs_api_routes_fine_tuning_get_fine_tuning_job_code-samples_typescript"
>

<CodeSample>

```typescript
import { Mistral } from "@mistralai/mistralai";

const mistral = new Mistral({
  apiKey: "MISTRAL_API_KEY",
});

async function run() {
  const result = await mistral.fineTuning.jobs.get({
    jobId: "c167a961-ffca-4bcf-93ac-6169468dd389",
  });

  console.log(result);
}

run();

```

</CodeSample>

</SectionContent>

<CodeSample>

```python
from mistralai import Mistral
import os


with Mistral(
    api_key=os.getenv("MISTRAL_API_KEY", ""),
) as mistral:

    res = mistral.fine_tuning.jobs.get(job_id="c167a961-ffca-4bcf-93ac-6169468dd389")

    # Handle response
    print(res)


```

<Operation>

<OperationTitleSection slot="title">

## <Pill variant="primary"><b>POST</b></Pill> /v1/fine\_tuning/jobs/\{job\_id\}/cancel \{#operation-jobs_api_routes_fine_tuning_cancel_fine_tuning_job\}

</OperationTitleSection>

<OperationSummarySection slot="summary">

_Cancel Fine Tuning Job_

</OperationSummarySection>

<OperationDescriptionSection slot="description">

Request the cancellation of a fine tuning job.

</OperationDescriptionSection>

<OperationCodeSamplesSection slot="code-samples">

<CodeSampleTabbedSection>

<CodeSampleTab
  slot="tab"
  id="operation-jobs_api_routes_fine_tuning_cancel_fine_tuning_job_code-samples_typescript"
  tags={{"codeSample":"typescript"}}
>

TypeScript

</CodeSampleTab>

<SectionContent
  slot="content"
  id="operation-jobs_api_routes_fine_tuning_cancel_fine_tuning_job_code-samples_typescript"
>

<CodeSample>

```typescript
import { Mistral } from "@mistralai/mistralai";

const mistral = new Mistral({
  apiKey: "MISTRAL_API_KEY",
});

async function run() {
  const result = await mistral.fineTuning.jobs.cancel({
    jobId: "6188a2f6-7513-4e0f-89cc-3f8088523a49",
  });

  console.log(result);
}

run();

```

</CodeSample>

</SectionContent>

<CodeSampleTab
  slot="tab"
  id="operation-jobs_api_routes_fine_tuning_cancel_fine_tuning_job_code-samples_python"
  tags={{"codeSample":"python"}}
>

Python

</CodeSampleTab>

<SectionContent
  slot="content"
  id="operation-jobs_api_routes_fine_tuning_cancel_fine_tuning_job_code-samples_python"
>

<CodeSample>

```python
from mistralai import Mistral
import os


with Mistral(
    api_key=os.getenv("MISTRAL_API_KEY", ""),
) as mistral:

    res = mistral.fine_tuning.jobs.cancel(job_id="6188a2f6-7513-4e0f-89cc-3f8088523a49")

    # Handle response
    print(res)


```

</CodeSample>

</SectionContent>

<CodeSampleTab
  slot="tab"
  id="operation-jobs_api_routes_fine_tuning_cancel_fine_tuning_job_code-samples_curl"

<Operation>

<OperationTitleSection slot="title">

## <Pill variant="primary"><b>POST</b></Pill> /v1/fine\_tuning/jobs/\{job\_id\}/start \{#operation-jobs_api_routes_fine_tuning_start_fine_tuning_job\}

</OperationTitleSection>

<OperationSummarySection slot="summary">

_Start Fine Tuning Job_

</OperationSummarySection>

<OperationDescriptionSection slot="description">

Request the start of a validated fine tuning job.

</OperationDescriptionSection>

<OperationCodeSamplesSection slot="code-samples">

<CodeSampleTabbedSection>

<CodeSampleTab
  slot="tab"
  id="operation-jobs_api_routes_fine_tuning_start_fine_tuning_job_code-samples_typescript"
  tags={{"codeSample":"typescript"}}
>

TypeScript

</CodeSampleTab>

<SectionContent
  slot="content"
  id="operation-jobs_api_routes_fine_tuning_start_fine_tuning_job_code-samples_typescript"
>

<CodeSample>

```typescript
import { Mistral } from "@mistralai/mistralai";

const mistral = new Mistral({
  apiKey: "MISTRAL_API_KEY",
});

async function run() {
  const result = await mistral.fineTuning.jobs.start({
    jobId: "56553e4d-0679-471e-b9ac-59a77d671103",
  });

  console.log(result);
}

run();

```

</CodeSample>

</SectionContent>

<CodeSampleTab
  slot="tab"
  id="operation-jobs_api_routes_fine_tuning_start_fine_tuning_job_code-samples_python"
  tags={{"codeSample":"python"}}
>

Python

</CodeSampleTab>

<SectionContent
  slot="content"
  id="operation-jobs_api_routes_fine_tuning_start_fine_tuning_job_code-samples_python"
>

<CodeSample>

```python
from mistralai import Mistral
import os


with Mistral(
    api_key=os.getenv("MISTRAL_API_KEY", ""),
) as mistral:

    res = mistral.fine_tuning.jobs.start(job_id="56553e4d-0679-471e-b9ac-59a77d671103")

    # Handle response
    print(res)


```

</CodeSample>

</SectionContent>

<CodeSampleTab
  slot="tab"
  id="operation-jobs_api_routes_fine_tuning_start_fine_tuning_job_code-samples_curl"
